  21 /* To generate a Unicode 3.2 CNS11643.TXT, take
  22    http://www.unicode.org/Public/Mappings/EASTASIA/OTHER/CNS11643.TXT
  23    and add the following lines (see Unicode 3.2 UNIHAN.TXT):
  24    0x12728  0x4EA0  #   <CJK Ideograph>
  25    0x1272F  0x51AB  #   <CJK Ideograph>
  26    0x12734  0x52F9  #   <CJK Ideograph>
  27  */
  28 
  29 /* The following table contains quite some big hole but I'm not sure whether
  30    it is a good idea to eliminate them.  The algorithm gets slower (has to
  31    use loops).  [And I'm too lazy in the moment.]
  32 
  33    The table can be generated using
  34 
  35    egrep '^0x1' CNS11643.TXT |
  36    awk '{print $1, $2}' | perl tab.pl
  37 
  38    where tab.pl is:
  39 
  40    ~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~
  41    $n=0;
  42    while (<>) {
  43      local($cns, $ucs4, %rest) = split;
  44      local($u)=hex($ucs4);
  45      local($c)=hex($cns)-0x12121;
  46      printf ("\n ") if ($n % 4 eq 0);
  47      ++$n;
  48      printf (" [0x%04x] = 0x%04x,",
  49              int($c / 256) * 94 + ($c & 0xff), $u);
  50    }
  51    printf ("\n");
  52    ~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~
  53 */

3673      printf (" [0x%04x] = \"\\x%02x\\x%02x\",", $u - 0xfe30,
3674              $c < 0x100 ? $c : int($c/256), $c < 0x100 ? 0 : $c&255);
